NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

NOTICES
FORM No. 151
(See Rule 315)
Members’ Voluntary Winding up
Notice of appointment of Liquidator pursuant to Section 516.
Name of the Company

: ORIENTAL MERCANTILE DISTRIBUTORS PRIVATE LIMITED.

Nature of Business

: Distributors, canvassers, commission-agents and brokers of all kinds of
pharmaceutical, medicinal, chemical, industrial and other preparations and articles.

Address of Registered Office

: New No. 9, Old No. 5, Chandrabagh Avenue, Mylapore, Chennai-600 004.

Name and Address of Liquidator : Shri Rajkumar Rajamani, New No. 9, Old No. 5, Chandrabagh Avenue, Mylapore,
Chennai-600 004.
Date of Appointment

: 17th March 2010.

By Whom Appointed

: By a special resolution of the members of Oriental Mercantile Distributors Private
Limited at their Meeting held on 17th March 2010.

RAJKUMAR RAJAMANI,
Liquidator.
ORIENTAL MERCANTILE DISTRIBUTORS PRIVATE LIMITED
Regd. Office: New No. 9, Old No. 5, Chandrabagh Avenue, Mylapore, Chennai-600 004.
Extracts of the Resolutions passed at the Extraordinary General Meeting of the Members of the Company held
on Wednesday, the 17th day of March 2010 at the Registered Office of the Company at New No. 9, Old No. 5,
Chandrabagh Avenue, Mylapore, Chennai-600 004.
Resolved that pursuant to Section 484(1)(b) of the Companies Act, 1956 and having regard to the declaration made by
the Board of directors dated 20th February 2010 and delivered to the Registrar of Companies under Section 488 of the
Companies Act, 1956, stating that the Company does not have any debts as at the date of the declaration, consent be and
is hereby accorded to voluntarily wind up the Company having its Registered Office at New No. 9, Old No. 5, Chandrabagh
Avenue, Mylapore, Chennai-600 004, with immediate effect.
Resolved further that Mr. R Rajkumar, Director, residing at New No. 9, Old No. 5, Chandrabagh Avenue, Mylapore,
Chennai-600 004, be and is hereby appointed as a Liquidator of the Company pursuant to the provisions of Section 490
of the Companies Act, 1956 at a total remuneration of Rs. 25,000 in addition to his costs, charges and expenses.
Further Resolved that Mr. R Rajkumar, the Liquidator be empowered to exercise all powers as provided in sub-clause
i to v of sub-section (2) of Section 457 of the Companies Act, 1956.
Resolved Further that Mr. R Rajkumar, Liquidator be and is hereby authorized to operate the banking account of the
company vide account number 0938201001728 with Canara Bank, Royapettah Branch, Chennai-600 014 and to draw,
accept, make and endorse any bill of exchange, hundi or promissory note in the name and on behalf of the company, with
the same effect with respect to the liability of the company as if the bill, hundi, or note had been drawn, accepted, made
or endorsed by or on behalf of the company in the course of its business as provided under Section 457(2) (iii) of the
Companies Act, 1956.
For Oriental Mercantile Distributors Private Limited,
Chennai,
23rd March 2010.

V K RAJAMANI,
Director.
